		graphical_culture = westerngfx
		color = { 255 255 153 }
		icon = 1
		heresy_icon = 6
		
		high_god_name = GOD_GOD
		
		crusade_name = "CRUSADE"
		piety_name = PIETY
		priest_title = PRIEST
		scripture_name = THE_BIBLE
		god_names = {
			GOD_GOD GOD_THE_LORD GOD_JESUS GOD_THE_BLESSED_VIRGIN
		}
		evil_god_names = {
			SATAN LUCIFER THE_DEVIL
		}
		
		character_modifier = {
			global_revolt_risk = -0.04
			general_opinion = 10
			church_opinion = 20
			castle_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.20
			temple_vassal_tax_modifier = -0.65
			land_organisation = 0.05
			temple_vassal_min_levy = -0.35
			temple_vassal_max_levy = -0.35
#			monthly_character_prestige = 1.00
#			monthly_character_piety = 0.50
			diplomacy = 2
			martial = -1
			stewardship = -1
			intrigue = 1
			fertility = -0.10
#			ai_zeal = 20
#			ai_honor = 20
#			ai_greed = 50
#			ai_rationality = -20
		}
		unit_home_modifier = {
			key = "OFF_RELIGION"
	
			light_cavalry_defensive = 0.20
			light_infantry_defensive = 0.20
			archers_defensive = 0.20
			land_morale = 0.30
		}
		
		can_call_crusade = yes
		can_excommunicate = yes
		can_grant_divorce = yes
		can_grant_invasion_cb = invasion
		can_grant_claim = yes
		can_have_antipopes = yes
		can_retire_to_monastery = yes
		investiture = yes
		priests_can_inherit = no
		short_reign_opinion_year_mult = 4 # The default in LI is 5

		# Christian open-minded (sectarian 0), can be married from the same group or civilization or related ones
		intermarry = adoptionist
		intermarry = apollinarist
		intermarry = arian
		intermarry = audianist 
		intermarry = docetist
		intermarry = mari_christ
		intermarry = monophysite
		intermarry = monothelite
		intermarry = nasrani
		intermarry = orthodox
		intermarry = sabellianist 
		intermarry = semipelagian
		intermarry = slavic_christian
		intermarry = unctionist
		intermarry = cathar_reformed
		intermarry = mari_christ_reformed
		intermarry = montanist_reformed
		intermarry = slavic_christian_reformed
		# ! Not in Christian civilization  but in Christian group: not to be married from sectarian 1 Christian faiths
		intermarry = celtic_christ
		intermarry = norse_christ
		intermarry = nasrani_reformed

		# Christian restrictive (sectarian 1), can be married from the same group or civilization or related ones
		intermarry = donatist 
		intermarry = fraticelli
		intermarry = iconoclast
		intermarry = marcionist 
		intermarry = melkite
		intermarry = montanist
		intermarry = nestorian
		intermarry = pelagian
		intermarry = solomonic_christ
		intermarry = valentinian 
		intermarry = waldensian
		intermarry = christian_populist_reformed
		intermarry = priscillian_reformed
		
		religious_clothing_head = 0
		religious_clothing_priest = 1
	}
